***порог.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порог.html>поро́г</a> (1335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*porgъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">threshold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*porʔgos</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*porg-o-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порог.html>поро́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poróg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порог.html>поро́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порог.html>поро́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порог.html>поро́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>threshold, doorstep</li>
<li>rapid <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">turbulent flow section in a river</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поро́говый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porógovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поро́жистый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poróžistyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***порода.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́да</a> (4333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poróda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> breed, kind, race, species, sort (all animals or plants of the same species or subspecies)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rock, layer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пуста́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustája <b>poróda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">barren rock, overburden, dirt, debris, waste rock</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:породить.html>породи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порождать.html>порожда́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порождать.html>порожда́ть</a> (8199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:породить.html>породи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порождать.html>порожда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poroždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:породить.html>породи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give birth</li>
<li>to beget, to cause, to entail, to generate</li>
<li>to engender, to give rise</li></ol>

***порожний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порожний.html>поро́жний</a> (21506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">порожьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porožĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from earlier <span class="Cyrs" lang="orv">пороздьнъ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="tr Latn">porozdĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*porzdьnъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:праздный.html>пра́здный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prázdnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порожний.html>поро́жний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poróžnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>empty <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">devoid of content</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́ж</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ний</b>

Зализняка — 2*a-.
<a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>Кра́ткая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> муж. р. предположительна.

***поросль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поросль.html>по́росль</a> (17767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поросль.html>по́росль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póroslʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порасти.html>по́росли</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>shoots, young growth, verdure</li>
<li>shrub</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> youth, young people</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>росль</b>

Зализняка).

***пороть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a> (11110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пороти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poroti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cut, rip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*porti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porótʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распороть.html>распоро́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпороть.html>вы́пороть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спороть.html>споро́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rip (a garment) at the seams, to unstitch
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распороть.html>распоро́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasporótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to flog, to flagellate
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпороть.html>вы́пороть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výporotʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>in expressions</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ахинея.html>ахине́ю</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:вздор.html>вздор</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:ерунда.html>ерунду́</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:чушь.html>чушь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>porótʹ</b> axinéju / vzdor / jerundú / čušʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to talk nonsense</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спороть.html>споро́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sporótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">unstitch</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">распа́рывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspáryvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***порох.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́рох</a> (8469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">порохъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poroxŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dust</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*porxъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прах.html>прах</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prax</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́рох</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pórox</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́роха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>пороха́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>порохо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gunpowder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́рох</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сухой.html>сухи́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">deržátʹ pórox suxím</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep one's powder dry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>пороха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú poroxa ne xvatájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he lacks the energy; he has not got it in him, he is not up to it</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>пороха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выдумать.html>вы́думает</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on poroxa ne výdumajet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he will never set the Thames on fire</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>па́хнет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́рохом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">páxnet póroxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is a smell of gunpowder in the air, war is in the air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понюхать.html>поню́хал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́роху</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>пороха</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on i ne ponjúxal póroxu (poroxa)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he hasn't experienced war</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порочить.html>поро́чить</a> (19960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порок.html>поро́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порочить.html>поро́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poróčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опорочить.html>опоро́чить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to defame, to discredit, to smear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порочить.html>поро́чить</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poróčitʹ</b> čʹjó-libo ímja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smear/discredit/tarnish smb's reputation; besmirch smb's name</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порочить.html>поро́чить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:показание.html>показа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свидетель.html>свиде́телей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poróčitʹ</b> pokazánija svidételej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to discredit the witnesses' testimony</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порочить.html>поро́чить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вывод.html>вы́воды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исследование.html>иссле́дования</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poróčitʹ</b> vývody isslédovanija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to discredit the findings of the investigation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порочность.html>поро́чность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poróčnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порочность.html>поро́чности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порочность.html>поро́чности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порочность.html>поро́чностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>depravity, viciousness</li>
<li>fallaciousness</li></ol>

***порочный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порочный.html>поро́чный</a> (13570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">порочныи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poročnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">порокъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porokŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ныи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Surface analysis: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порок.html>поро́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порочный.html>поро́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poróčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>immoral, vicious, depraved, wanton</li>
<li>faulty, defective, flawed, fallacious</li></ol>

***порт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порт.html>порт</a> (2316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First dated 1702, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">port</i> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Port</i>, finally from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">portus</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порт.html>порт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">port</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порт.html>по́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порт.html>по́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порт.html>порто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>port, harbor</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>по́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́в<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-портативн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***портить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:портить.html>по́ртить</a> (5484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пъртити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pŭrtiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pъrtiti</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">portnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портить.html>по́ртить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pórtitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испортить.html>испо́ртить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попортить.html>попо́ртить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spoil, to ruin, to mar, to damage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to corrupt, to spoil, to deflower (virgins)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пъртъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pŭrtŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">piece of cloth (sg)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">portnój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портно́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портны́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портны́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портниха.html>портни́ха</a></b>)
